[3:05:42] Queen_Tiem: @morpheusx2001 you're acting like being 2nd place is the same as being 10th. To get 2nd place in playoffs is precisely 1 series easier than getting first place. Winning msi as a 2nd place seed after you qualify takes at least 2 more bo5s than it used to. So a team that made playoff finals in the old format needs to win 1 less series in the old format to win msi than they do in the new format if they lose their regional finals. Thats pretty fucking simple math
